<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:inhouden.html>inhouden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to contain, to encompass, to include</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mean, to imply</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to contain/restrain oneself</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:inkomen.html>inkomen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to come in</li>
<li>to <a href = vnd.unilang:warm.html>warm</a> up when starting an activity</li></ol>

***inkt.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:inkt.html>inkt</a> (7719)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">inct</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ink</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">encaustum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the red ink used by Roman and Greek rulers to sign documents</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">encaustus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">paint technique using wax burning</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἔγκαυστον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">énkauston</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">burned-in</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἐν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a></span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">in</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-tr tr Latn">kaíō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">burn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">encaustiek</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ink</i>.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:inkt.html>inkt</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ink</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vis.html>vis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">squid</span>, marine <a href = vnd.unilang:mollusk.html>mollusk</a> of the superorder Decapodiformes or more generally (including octopuses) of the class Cephalopoda.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">in</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leveren.html>leveren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to deliver</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***innuendo.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:innuendo.html>innuendo</a> (104980)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">innuendō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">by nodding</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ablative singular form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">innuendum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a nodding</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gerund.html>gerund</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">innuō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I give a nod</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:innuendo.html>innuendo</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">innuendoes</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">innuendos</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">innuendis</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A derogatory hint or reference to a person or thing. An implication, intimation or insinuation.
<dl><dd><i>She made a devious <b><a href = vnd.unilang:innuendo.html>innuendo</a></b> about her husband, who <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> embarrassed.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">logic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A rhetorical device with an omitted, but obvious conclusion, made to increase the force of an argument.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Part of a pleading in <a href = vnd.unilang:cases.html>cases</a> of libel and slander, pointing out what and whom <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> meant by the libellous matter or description.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">innuendous</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:innuendo.html>innuendo</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">innuendos</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">innuendoing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">innuendoed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To interpret (something libellous or slanderous) in <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> of what <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> implied.
<ul><li><b>1894</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:frank.html>Frank</a> Towers <a href = vnd.unilang:cooper.html>Cooper</a>, <i>A Handbook of the Law of Defamation and Verbal Injury</i> (page 119)
<dl><dd>A statement that a person's presence at a certain club may be "irksome," may be <b>innuendoed</b> that the person <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> of such bad character as not to be a fit associate with honourable <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:inpakken.html>inpakken</a> (3647)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pakken.html>pakken</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pack up, to load <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> into a package</li>

***inshallah.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:inshallah.html>inshallah</a> (57143)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">إِنْ شَاءَ ٱللَٰه</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ʾin šāʾa llāh</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:inshallah.html>inshallah</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> willing; <a href = vnd.unilang:deo.html>Deo</a> volente; expressing the speaker’s wish for a given future event to occur, especially in a Muslim country or Islamic context.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> will sign the contract tomorrow, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:inshallah.html>inshallah</a></b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>In many contexts, including military <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a>, the expression <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sarcastic, suggesting that the speaker <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> no interest in making the future event occur (thus, it will only occur if <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:steps.html>steps</a> in and wills it).</li>
<li>In Arab countries <a href = vnd.unilang:inshallah.html>inshallah</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often added to any sentence in the future tense. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> to show that the future event <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not assured and if <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a>'s will <a href = vnd.unilang:steps.html>steps</a> in, it will not happen. I wish the event <a href = vnd.unilang:happens.html>happens</a>, but I don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> have it all in my hands and unpredictable can happen. I wish it <a href = vnd.unilang:happens.html>happens</a>, but if it's not <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a>'s will, it will not happen.</li></ul>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:inslaan.html>inslaan</a> (9212)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slaan.html>slaan</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:inslaan.html>inslaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to shatter, to break with force</li>
<li>to turn into, to follow (e.g. a different path or a corner)</li>
<li>to make provision for (e.g. a feast)</li>
<li>to strike with force (e.g. lightning)</li></ol>
